## 3. Panel Designs

---

## Summary

This comprehensive design document provides:

1. **Complete Architecture**: Component hierarchy, state flow, and data flow diagrams
2. **Detailed Workflows**: 5 major workflows with step-by-step processes
3. **Panel Designs**: 5 fully-specified panels with layouts and interactions
4. **Role Adaptations**: 3 role-specific UI configurations
5. **Interaction States**: Loading, empty, error, and success states for all panels
6. **Keyboard Shortcuts**: Complete navigation system with ~100 shortcuts
7. **Responsive Design**: 6 layout variants from full desktop to minimum viable
8. **Visual Design System**: Colors, typography, spacing, icons, and status indicators

All designs use ASCII art for easy version control and are structured for immediate implementation by developers.
